 jahaan kan-kan main banke bihari basate hai, vahaan ab abir or gulaal ud rahaa he
 Anyway, Holi of Mathura is famous for its special style across the world
 phir vah chaahe barasaane kii latoomaar holi ho yaa phool kii holi yaa ladduon kii holi yaa phir abir or gulaal kii holi ho
 radha-krishna's love mind should have the color of Holi on every Brijwasi
 phaguna ke maheene main braj kii aabhohawaa main masti or ullas bharaa hota he
 People here start celebrating Holi only after Basant Panchami
 vrundavan, nandagaanv or barsaanaa samet anya ilaake main holi khub kheli jaati he
 The surrounding environment becomes like this, as if everyone is mesmerized and is dancing on Krishna's flute and blowing abir-gulal
 mathurake rajaadhiraj bazaar sthit dwarkadhish mandir main dhol nagaadon kii dhooma se yah jaahir ho jaataa he ki yahaan horiyaaron (holi khilne waalon) kii hode he
 Holi is played in the color of turmeric before the Aarti of Dwarkadhish Lord here from 10 to 11 am
 natwar nagar ke natkhat andaaj ko yaad karte hue yahaan horiyaare khub naachte or jhuumate hai
 Pandit Laxman Chand of Dwarkadhish temple said that by the grace of Bankebihari, Brajbhoomi is prosperous and prosperous
 unki hi dein he ki yahaan har brajvasi har vakt muskuraataa rahata he

 is dauraan ham radha or krishna kii seva main sab kuch arpit kar dete hai or bade dhoomdhaam se holi manaate hai

 karnataka ke lokayukta justise bhaskar raav ke khilaaf vidhansabha main mahabhiyog kii prakriya sharu ho gai he taaki istifa na dene par ade lokayukta justise bhaskar raav ko unke pad se hataaya ja sake
 He will be the first such Lokayukta of the country to be removed from his post by impeachment
 darasal, lokayukta justise bhaskar raav pichley teen maheene se daftar nahin aa rahe, jabase unke bete asina raav par lokayukta red kaa dar dikhaakar sarkari adhikariyon se taqariban 100 karod rupee phiroti vasuulne kaa aarope laga he
 After the uproar in this case, the government formed a special investigation team under the supervision of IG level officer Kamal Pant, who arrested Ashwin Rao as well as Joint Commissioner Syed Riyaz and a friend posted in the Lokayukta office and sent to jail
 Had given
 zaahir he ki lokayukta daftar or unke sarkari nivas se chal rahe is racket kii jaankaree lokayukta justise bhaskar raav ko thi
 He has also been questioned by the SIT in this regard, but due to his holding a constitutional post, there are some legal complications in taking action against him
 vahiin, duusari taraf itani fajihat hone ke baavjood bhaskar raav ne ab tak istipha nahin diya he
 However, every possible effort was made to remove them from the government
 aise main justise bhaskar raav ko unke pad se hataane ke aakhri vikalp ke taur par mahabhiyog prastaav kaa sahaara liya gaya, lekin isse pehle prakriya ko aasaan banane ke liye kanoon main sanshodhan bhi kiya gaya he
 The Lokayukta's powers will remain suspended till the Chief Justice's powers, if a third member of the Legislative Assembly gives a written proposal to the Speaker and the Speaker approves it and sends it to the Chief Justice of Karnataka to remove the Lokayukta through impeachment with the help of the new law
 Investigation report will not come
 tippaniyan As soon as the Chief Justice comes to the request letter to get the speaker examined, he will have to form a committee of 3 judges and he will have to examine and submit his report to the speaker within three months
 agar report main lokayukta ko doshi paaya gaya to donon sadanon main mahabhiyog prastaav paarit kar lokayukta ko hataaya ja saktaa he
 The Karnataka Legislative Assembly currently has 225 members, that is, 75 members need signatures to start the process of impeachment motion
 jabaki vipaksh ke paas 80 ke aasapaas vidhayak hai, jedies or bijepi donon milkaar
 In such a situation, both these opposition parties completed the signature campaign and handed it over to Karnataka Assembly Speaker Kogadu Thimappa
 thimppa ne bataaya ki nae kanoon ke praavdhaanon ke mutabik wo ab is prastaav ko karnataka hai court ke mukhya nyaayadhish ko aage kii karrwai ke liye saunp denge
 In fact, Lokayukta Justice Bhaskar Rao has not been coming to office for the last three months, since his son Ashwin Rao has been accused of extorting about Rs 100 crore from government officials by showing fear of Lokayukta Red
 is maamle main hangaamaa uthne par sarkaar ne aiji level ke adhikari camel pant kii dekharekh main ek vishesh jaanch dal kaa gathan kiya tha, jisane asina raav ke saath-saath lokayukta daftar main tainaat sanyukt ayukta sayed riyaaz or unke ek mitra ko giraftaar kar jail bhej diya tha
 It is clear that Lokayukta Justice Bhaskar Rao was aware of this racket running from Lokayukta office and his official residence
 unase bhi esaiti ne is babat poochtacha kii he, lekin sanvaidhanik pad par asin hone kii vajah se unke khilaaf karrwai karne main kuch kanoonee pechidgiyaan aa rahi hai
 On the other hand, Bhaskar Rao has not resigned so far despite being so upset
 haalanki sarkaar kii taraf se unhen hataane kii har mumkin koshish kii gai
 In such a situation, impeachment motion was resorted to as the last option to remove Justice Bhaskar Rao from his post, but before that the law has also been amended to make the process easier
 nae kanoon ke sahare lokayukta ko mahabhiyog ke jariye hataane ke liye vidhansabha ke ek tihaai sadsy agar likhit prastaav spikar ko den or spikar use manjuur kar karnataka hoicourt ke mukhya nyaayadhish ko bhej den to lokayukta kii shaktiyaan tab tak nilambit rahengi, jab tak chif justise kii jaanch report na aa jaae
 The comments chif justise ke paas jaise hi spikar kaa jaanch karwaane kaa anurodh patr aayega, unhen 3 maujuud jajon kii samiti banani hogi or use jaanch kar teen maheene ke andar apni report spikar ko saunpny hogi
 If the Lokayukta is found guilty in the report, the Lokayukta can be removed by passing a motion of impeachment in both the houses
 philhal karnataka vidhansabha main 225 sadsy hai, yani mahabhiyog prastaav kii prakriya shuru karne ke liye 75 sadasyon ke hastakshar chahie

 biometrics data ke durupyog kii koshish kii ek ghatana ko sahi maanate hai hue unic identification athurity of india (yuidiai) ne ravivaar ko kaha ki register kiye gaye logon kii sabhi suchanaaen surakshit hai
 This statement of UIDAI has come when the news of the breach in the base data is coming again and again
 electronics evam iti mantralay ne ek bayaan main kaha, ’apni tarah kaa yah pehla maamla he jo yuidiai kii aantarik suraksha pranali kii pakad main aa gaya or uske saath hi aadhaar adhinium ke tahat karrwai shuru kar di gai he
 According to the Ministry, UIDAI has said that it has taken note of these reports in view of misinformation such as breach of base data, misuse of biometrics, breach of privacy and creation of parallel data base in various print and social media over the last few days
 And she wants to insist that there is no dent in the Aadhaar's UIDAI database and that UIDAI has the personal data of the people Ta is absolutely safe
 ’mantralay ke mutabik, 'yuidiai data ke transfar or hosting ke liye sabase unnat ancripshap takanic kaa prayog kiya jaataa he
 According to the statement, 'as a result, there has been no news of any citizen's data being breached by UIDAI in the last seven years

 It includes all transactions of back accounts through digital medium
 nae niyam ke mutabik ek graahak kii jimmedaari shunya ho jaati he, yadi anaadhikrut len-dein bank kii galati se hua ho
 This includes all things like fraud, negligence, rejection
 iske liye bank ko report karnaa bhi jaruri nahin hai
 Even if both the bank or the customer is not at fault during the third party transaction, there is a flaw in the system and the customer informs the bank about this unauthorized transaction within three working days, even then its liability is considered to be zero i
e
 to the bank Full money has to be returned
 anaadhikrut lenden main ek graahak kii deyta do tarah ke maamalon main alag-alag hoti he
 If the customer has been negligent, for example, he has shared the information about his payment with anyone and has not informed it to the bank, then in this case the customer will have to bear the entire loss
 kisi anaadhikrut lenden main bank yaa graahak donon hi galati na ho, magar graahak ke report kar dene baad bhi system main deree ho (chaar se saat kaarobaari dinon kii), to aisi sthiti main bhi graahak kii deyta simit maani jaati he
 If there is a delay of more than seven working days in giving the information of the report, then the liability of the customer will be based on the policy approved by the bank's board

[endif] kitaab:pishan flower: 'seven stories of dirrangement'publication:alef book companykimat:495 rupepanne:200insaan khaamiyon kaa pulinda he
 The gray shadows of life separate him from God
 iske baavjood har koi parfect bananaa chahta he
 Often, in our thinking process, we are not able to easily accept the rise and flourish of immoral values
 ham sab ek saamaajik duniya main rahete hai jahaan dusron kii najaron main aakarshak bane rahane ke liye bheetar ke pashu ko chipa lene kaa rivaaj he
 This animal is part of our brain
 yah hameshaa aanshik rup se hamaare bheetar sakriy rahata he or lucatipi kheltaa rahata he
 Cyrus Mistry's book Passion Flower is a collection of seven such stories in which people feel the dark side of life, recognize them and struggle to overcome them
 saaton kahaniyon ke mukhya kirdaaron main bahut kuch aapke or hamaare jaisaa he
 Due to this connection, writing keeps you connected to these stories
 haalanki kissagoi kii raftaar kuch dhimi he, lekin aage badhane ke saath kirdaar viksit hote jate hai
 In these stories, sometimes the sequence of times varies randomly
 aap saath-saath beete hue kal or vartmaan main uski jhalak ko dekh pate hai
 The first story is 'percy'
 yah ek skool kii padhai bich main chhod dene vaale ek aise shaks kii kahani he jo apane biimaar pita ke gramophone ke jariye kai saal baad sangeet se ishk kar baithta he
 People around him used to look at him with pity and derision
 lekin kai saal tak yon utpeedan kii vednaa or tiraskaar jhelane ke baad vah khud ko khush rakhana sikh jaataa he
 He does not find life as difficult as before
 uski jindagi badal jaati he ek bhoot se milane ke baad
 Bhoot, who had an effective advice for him
 ummid se labarej ek or kahani he 'anexpected gres and finali choped dil'
 It is about those two women who are facing the same pain arising from different state of mind
 ek nai naveli maa he priti, jo 'anidra main akelaa' mahasoos karti he
 This restless and destitute woman is scared of the idea that she will strangulate her 'little Demon Prawns' and kill her
 vah apane pati ko vyabhichaar kii sajaa dene ke liye 'midia' kii bhi madad leti he
 The other woman is the prolific cook Jasintha, who is tortured by her own intoxicated brother, his 'witch' wife, and his past
 baad main donon apane apane 'pashu' par kaabo paane ke upaay khoj lete hai
 Relationships never last
 vakt kii rassiyaan un par apane achche-bure nishaan chhod hi jaati hai
 The story 'two Angry Men' is the story of two old friends, whose friendship and meaning change with time
 jaise-jaise kahani aage badhati he aapako ilm hota he ki dosti or vyapaar main se jeet ek kii hoti he
 'late for Dinner' is the story of a Parsi couple who are waiting for their daughter to go to a party and during this time the pages of their own life begin to turn and scary memories of the past are on their minds
 'pishan flower' main bhi tanaavpurn rishton, swarthpurna faislon or matibhram kii kahani bayaan kii gai he
 Anand is a botany expert
 vah apane sapane puraa karnaa chahta he
 But he is so immersed in himself that he despises every person who interrupts his mission
 apni mahatvakankshaayen puri karne ke liye vah apni namrata ko daanv par laga detaa he
 He also becomes cruel against those who do not really wish to harm him
 lekin baad main use is baat kaa afsos hota he
 The last story is 'bokha'
 vah ek ladke kii kahani he jisaki swaarthee maa uski besahaara garlfriend seraphina ko nuksaan pahunchane par amada he
 The specialty of Mistry's stories is that you are left to interpret
 vah har baar parpanrik clymex nahin dete
 Rather, we leave its meaning on our mind
 unki kahaniyon kaa ahm sila yahi he ki sab kahaniyon kaa ant khushnuma nahin hota or yah ek sachai he

 yah us asaadhaaran yatra ke bare main he jisamen jindagi ko uske saamaanya dhoosar rangon ke saath swikaarna hota he

 is akeli bikri se reliance inphra ke karj main kareeb 25 fisadi kii kami aegi

 AIADMK simbel zabt hone ke baad donon guton ne apni alag-alag party bana lee he, jise chunaav ayog kii manzuri bhi mil gai he

 darasal- shashikala or panniraselvam ke bich AIADMK ke simbel ko lekar vivaad ke baad buudhvaar ko chunaav ayog ne party ke chunaav chihn 'do pattiyaan' ko zabt kar liya

 (inputs IANS se bhi) Telecom operator Reliance Communication (rcom) is going to discontinue voice call service from 1 December
 saal ke ant tak graahak duusare network kaa ruukh kar sakate hai
 On Friday, the Telecom Authority of India (TRAI) gave this information
 pitiai kii khabar ke mutabik, sabhi telecom operators ko tri kii ore se jari soochna main bataaya ki 31 oktober 2017 ko arcom ne kaha, ' reliance communication limited (RCL) apane graahakon ko keval 4G data sarvice hi uplabdh kara saktaa he
 Due to this, we will not be able to provide voice service to our subscribers from 1 December 2017
 'rcom ne TRAI ko jaankaree di ki wo aath telecom cirkil- andhra-pradesh, haryana, maharashtra, upi east or west, tamil nadu, karnataka or kerala main apni 2G or 4G sevaayen uplabdh karaata he
 The Anil Ambani-led company informed TRAI that the company was upgrading the CDMA network of its merged company Sistema Shyam Teleservices
 taaki company dilli, rajasthan, upi west, tamilnadu, kerala, karnataka, pashchim bengal, gujarat or kolkata main 4G sarvice uplabdh kara sake
 TRAI said that Rcom has released all the necessary information regarding porting of voice calls along with porting to other networks
 tri ne Rcom ko kisi bhi porting request ko riject nahin karne kaa aadesh diya he or sabhi telecom companiyon se31 disambar 2017tak Rcom sabsakribers ke request except karne ko kaha he
